       Graduate Electronics/Computer Science Software Engineer
      </li>

    <div class="md:tw-container">
     <h1 class="tw-text-employer-500 tw-text-balance" itemprop="title">
      Graduate Electronics/Computer Science Software Engineer
     </h1>
     <h2 class="tw-w-3/4 tw-text-base tw-font-semibold tw-text-gray-700">
     </h2>
    </div>
    <div class="tw-flex tw-gap-12 md:tw-container">
     <div class="tw-flex-[3] tw-min-w-0">
      <div class="job-description mb20">
       <div class="my34" style="border-bottom: 2px #EEF0F3 solid">
       </div>
       <div class="body-content">
        <h3>
         About the role
        </h3>
        <p>
         <strong>
          A unique opportunity to join a growing new company developing some exciting products in the 5G mobile infrastructure space.
         </strong>
         As a recent graduate you would be joining an R&amp;D team involved in the design, development and manufacture of these products.
        </p>
        <div class="right-image">
         <img src="https://images.gradcracker.com/eyJrZXkiOiJhc3NldHNcL2VtcGxveWVyc1wvMTIyMVwveXVrc1EwMTF1bHRzRDRHbUZaNnU0dXNZdGZZbURVVTNwRXpmQjdoMi5qcGciLCJlZGl0cyI6eyJyZXNpemUiOnsid2lkdGgiOjQwMH0sInRvRm9ybWF0IjoianBlZyIsImpwZWciOnsicXVhbGl0eSI6NjB9fX0=?signature=9275b60fd7f546293e13b2f181e1ef9d38ef3c07afcca2cd54e870857c2a0b77"/>
        </div>
        <p>
         The role will be able to take the skills learnt during your degree and apply them to real world applications. Working from requirements you will be expected to develop all forms of software across the full suite; from firmware on microprocessors such as the Raspberry PI, with code written in C and/or Python, all the way through to GUI development using rapid development tools such as NodeRED.
        </p>
        <p>
         The role will involve both working as a critical member of the team, but equally you will be expected to work independently and to set direction for others. If you are a passionate problem solver, enjoy a challenge, and want to develop, this is the role for you!
        </p>
        <h3>
         Roles/Responsibility
        </h3>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Management of functional and non-functional requirements deriving the HLD &amp; LLD designs for software development.
         </li>
         <li>
          Operate in an agile/scrum environment with incremental and regular delivery.
         </li>
         <li>
          Software development using a CI/CD pipeline.
         </li>
         <li>
          Development of test environments, facilitating automated testing.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <h3>
         Education Qualifications:
        </h3>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Bachelor's degree in Computer Science or similar STEM discipline, or proven development experience.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <h3>
         Desired Characteristics &amp; Technical Expertise:
        </h3>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Full software life cycle development.
         </li>
         <li>
          Variety of embedded platforms.
         </li>
         <li>
          Experience in Windows, Linux OS.
         </li>
         <li>
          Web development, HTML, CSS, Java Script, MQTT.
         </li>
         <li>
          Front end/GUI building &amp; app development.
         </li>
         <li>
          CI/CD with version control and code repositories such as GitHub.
         </li>
         <li>
          Scrum team development using Agile project management.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <h3>
         Business Acumen:
        </h3>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Skilled in breaking down problems, documenting problem statements and estimating efforts.
         </li>
         <li>
          Understands the importance of software quality and the impact of product quality and the risk of brand damage.
         </li>
         <li>
          Ability to analyse design options and deliver the best solutions into the products.
         </li>
         <li>
          Awareness of competitors and industry trends.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <h3>
         Personal Attributes:
        </h3>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Excellent oral and written communications skills.
         </li>
         <li>
          Effective interpersonal/extensive team building skills.
         </li>
         <li>
          Able to problem solve, finding effective solutions.
         </li>
         <li>
          Pushing self and team results through team spirit.
         </li>
         <li>
          A can do and willing attitude.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <h3>
         Benefits
        </h3>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Competitive starting salary:
          <strong>
           £30,000
          </strong>
         </li>
         <li>
          Company pension
         </li>
         <li>
          25 days' annual leave
         </li>
         <li>
          Ongoing training and development opportunities, to allow you to
          <strong>
           reach your full potential
          </strong>
         </li>
         <li>
          Informal dress code and excellent work/life balance
         </li>
         <li>
          Reimbursement towards a professional membership.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Security Clearance:
         </strong>
         The company develops solutions for military applications and staff within the business are expected to be able to be security cleared as and when required.
        </p>
        <div class="tw-inline-flex tw-items-center tw-cursor-pointer" onclick="Livewire.dispatch('modal.open', { component: 'modals.feedback-pledge' })">
         <svg aria-hidden="true" class="tw-flex-none tw-w-12 tw-h-12 tw-mr-2 tw-text-employer-500" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" viewbox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
          <path d="M9 12l2 2 4-4m6 2a9 9 0 11-18 0 9 9 0 0118 0z" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round">
          </path>
         </svg>
         <div>
          <div class="tw-text-sm tw-font-semibold">
           We've signed the Gradcracker feedback pledge.
          </div>
          <div class="tw-text-xs tw-font-normal">
           (This means that we will supply feedback if requested after an interview.)
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

        </p>
